North China Japanese Army Holds Large-Scale Exercise, Simulating the Occupation of Beiping; Several Thousand Civilian Houses Preemptively Requisitioned for Use; Beiping Taken as the Target for Seizure During the Exercise; Celebration Held in Assumption of Victory After the Exercise

Tianjin Dispatch: The large-scale exercise of the Japanese Army in North China is nearing its end. Infantry Brigade Commander stationed in Beiping, Kawahara Masami, specially came to Tianjin with his adjutant, Onoguchi, on the 22nd to attend the preparatory meeting for the large-scale exercise convened by Japanese Army Commander Tashiro. The meeting was held at 10:00 AM on the 22nd at the Japanese barracks in Hai Guang Temple. Independent Artillery Regiment Commander Suzuki stationed in Qinhuangdao, Captain Nakajima of Shanhaiguan, Pinbe of Tangshan, and Kagawa of Tanggu all rushed to attend. It was decided that the troops stationed in Tangyu, Australia, and Chang would mobilize from the 24th, first gathering in the Tianjin suburbs of Hai Xia, Xian Shui Gu, Xiao Liu Zhuang, and Da Zhi Gu. At 6:00 AM on the 26th, the Mutaguchi 1st Infantry Regiment near Beiping and the Katada Battalion in Fengtai will simultaneously conduct separate regimental exercises. That evening, after the meeting, each commander returned to their defense area to make preparations. Kawahara then took the night train to Tanggu and other places for inspection and to give instructions. From the 22nd, the Japanese Army Headquarters dispatched staff officers Keii, Ada, and Kabei to the suburbs of Pingfengtonglu to requisition civilian houses, directly contacting local township chiefs and police chiefs. Several thousand civilian houses were requisitioned in areas such as Tongzhou, Fengtai, outside Xizhimen in western Beiping, and Babaoshan. More than 400 civilian houses were also requisitioned in the Tianjin suburbs of Xian Shui Gu, Xiao Liu Zhuang, and Da Zhi Gu. Each civilian house was required to have a kang (heated brick bed) and be located on a street with important traffic. Each house was required to accommodate five soldiers, each with a daily rental fee of one jiao. From the 22nd, all homeowners were required to vacate, but two men were required to remain in each house to provide temporary services and were responsible for guarding any items left behind by the Japanese soldiers during the exercise. Although the residents were extremely unwilling, opposition was ineffective. For days, in the Tianjin suburbs of Da Zhi Gu, men, women, and children carried their belongings and came to Tianjin in an endless stream, in a very miserable state. The ignorant people spread rumors, causing widespread panic, believing that something terrible was about to happen. The Chahar-Suiyuan Pacification Headquarters previously sent Chen Zhongfu to Tianjin to consult with Japanese Army Chief of Staff Hashimoto on this matter, requesting that they consider social order and tranquility. If there was a need to use houses for barracks, the government would find public property or factories and shops, which would save costs and make access easier. Hashimoto said that the matter had already been determined by the operations section of the military headquarters and could not be changed, but he would pay attention to restraining the troops as much as possible and occupying fewer civilian houses. As for the operational plan for this large-scale exercise, the Japanese military headquarters officially notified our Chahar-Suiyuan Pacification Headquarters to inform all agencies. From the 26th to the 28th, separate regimental exercises will be held, combining various special forces, with the Mutaguchi and Kayashima 1st and 2nd Infantry Regiments as units, conducting operations in the suburbs of Pingjin, using new-style chemical warfare equipment, tanks, and armored car teams. Each regiment will have approximately 2,500 participants. The 29th will be a rest day. From the 30th to the 31st, regimental confrontation exercises will be held in Fengtai, Lugouqiao, Changxindian, and Tongzhou near Beiping. The 1st and 2nd Regiments will engage in encounters, defenses, and battles along the Pingjin and Pinghan roads. All troops under the Kawahara Brigade will participate, with Kawahara personally supervising, commanding, and issuing orders. November 1st will be a rest day. On November 2nd, Nam Dai will go to Tongzhou with all the staff of the military headquarters to set up the headquarters. From 5:00 AM that morning, a dawn battle will be held. More than 70% of the Japanese army in North China will participate, with Beiping and Fengtai as the targets for seizure. The Mutaguchi Regiment, combined with various chemical warfare units, will be the defending force, while the Kayashima and Suzuki Regiments and the Air Force will be the attacking force, demonstrating the latest-style equipment and combat power of the entire army. On November 3rd, a night battle and reconnaissance battle will be held. The hypothetical strategy is that Beiping, under superior defense, encounters pressure from the air and land forces and destruction of transportation, falling into isolation. Communication between Pinghan, Pingsui, and Pingjin is completely cut off. On the morning of November 4th, due to the successful special activities of the volunteer soldiers in civilian clothes outside Xizhimen, Beiping feels threatened and collapses. This section of the exercise is the main item arranged by the operations section of this session. Therefore, immediately after the exercise on that day, a celebration of the assumed victory will be held at Babaoshan in the suburbs of Beiping. A military parade will be held under the grand review of the Japanese representative. Rest in the afternoon and camp in western Beiping. The exercise will end on November 5th, and the troops will return to their defenses one after another. The intention of this exercise is a routine seasonal matter, but the scale of the mobilization and the certainty of the purpose cannot help but make one tremble for North China. (22nd) Beiping Dispatch: The Japanese garrison army in North China is scheduled to hold its autumn large-scale exercise from the 26th of this month to the 4th of November. First, there will be separate regimental exercises, then confrontational exercises, expanding into brigade exercises, and finally divisional exercises. Because the exercise time is long and the number of people is large, the lodging locations must be determined in advance. On the 21st, the Japanese side sent Infantry Major Okamura Katsumi, Accounting Officer Matsuo Kanji, Medical Officer Yakumoto Seishi, and Captain Adjutant Kono Matasaburo, together with Zhao Yafan, a member of the Second Section of the Beiping Municipal Public Security Bureau, to inspect lodging locations in the suburbs of Beiping and negotiate with local chambers of commerce to purchase firewood, white soybeans, pork, cabbage, and other necessary items, and to hire laborers to provide catering. On the first day (26th), the advance personnel of the Japanese army will arrive at Dongba to make arrangements. On the 27th, more than 2,300 Japanese officers and soldiers stationed in Fengtai and Tongxian will arrive in batches. On the 28th, they will depart to conduct exercises in Gongzhufen, Songjiafen, Sanshengci, and other places in eastern Beiping, and camp separately. On the 29th and 30th, they will continue to conduct exercises in Balizhuang, Dalincun, Tianlingsi in the southern suburbs, and Bailingguan, Yuanguangsi, Caishenmiao, and Wanshoushan in the western suburbs. On the last day, a military parade will be held in Babaoshan in Wanping County, with Japanese Commander Tashiro participating. At 10:00 AM that morning, all 200-plus officers will have a luncheon at the Natural History Museum and invite representatives from our military and political circles to participate. In total, there will be four days of exercises within the boundary of Beiping City: the 26th and 27th of this month and the 3rd and 4th of next month. In addition to the exercise of guns, Beiping's ancient city will be the assumed target of attack. This exercise, in addition to what they call ordinary military education, implies an on-the-ground survey of the terrain. In order to prevent citizens from being alarmed by the sounds at the time, the Beiping Municipal Public Security Bureau will issue a notice to inform the public and order each district team to stop resting during these ten days to provide protection. Furthermore, last month, for the sake of the exercise, the Japanese side requested to borrow our civilian houses at that time. The authorities stated that our country has no such custom. Although it is common for the Japanese, it is unprecedented in our country. In order to avoid misunderstandings, the Japanese side was asked not to adopt this approach. As a result, it is heard that our government will rent accommodations on their behalf. Battalion Commander Tanimura of the Japanese artillery regiment went to Fengtai from Beiping on the 22nd to negotiate with the local authorities. In addition to renting houses to be used as campsites for the Japanese army going to Beiping for exercises, they also rented a civilian house in Xinglong Hutong for the Japanese army in Tianjin to use. (22nd)

New Facilities of the Gansu Provincial Government: Training Accounting Personnel, Relieving Refugees After Robbery, Constructing the Gansu-Xinjiang Highway, and Preparing to Plant Trees Along the Yellow River

Lanzhou Dispatch: Provincial Chairman Yu Xuezhong believes that the accounting personnel in various county bureaus are extremely important to the consolidation of local finances. In order to select and assist economic talents to consolidate local finances, he intends to prepare for the establishment of an accounting personnel training institute to engage in training in order to assign them to work in various counties. All students will be recruited through examinations and limited to high school graduates. After graduating from training, they will first practice in Gaolan County and then be assigned. He ordered the person in charge to properly draft regulations for implementation. The Provincial Affairs Conference has passed it, and preparations have already begun.

Minlin and other counties in this province have been ravaged by bandits for a long time. Resources have been plundered, livelihoods have been cut off, and people are gathering and crying, pitifully hungry and cold. Provincial Chairman Yu decided to implement emergency relief to provide assistance. He submitted a resolution to the Provincial Affairs Conference, ordering the Relief Committee to allocate 7,000 yuan to Minxian, 1,500 yuan to Lintao, 2,000 yuan to Lintan, 3,000 yuan to Weiyuan, and 3,000 yuan to Zhangxian from the central relief funds, and ordered them to be remitted separately for emergency relief.

Regarding the construction of the Gansu-Xinjiang Highway, Chairman Yu previously telegraphed the Economic Commission to send survey team leader Liu Rusong to lead a team to the west. The survey of the Lanwu section has been completed. The construction costs required have been repeatedly telegraphed to the Economic Commission for allocation in order to start construction. Approval has been received to allocate 200,000 yuan in construction funds in the 25th year to start construction on the Gaolan to Yongdeng section. It is planned to start from Hekou on the north bank of the Yellow River, 90 li west of Lanzhou, along the east bank of the Zhuanglang River to Yongdeng County, with a total length of more than 140 li. For all construction matters, the Provincial Government has hired Liu Rusong as the chief engineer, responsible for carrying out supervision and guidance, and established a Gansu-Xinjiang Highway Engineering Office, which has been organized and officially established.

The afforestation project along the Yellow River in Gansu Province is extremely important for downstream flooding and safety. The Provincial Government has commissioned Fan Shuxin to survey the actual situation. However, the implementation period and method of afforestation must be tested first before implementation. It has been decided to conduct a trial planting in another area using the stem-burying method in late autumn this year. After the trial is successful, implementation will begin next year according to the planned plan. As for the trial area, Yantan and other places have been selected, and work will begin soon.

The section of the roadbed at Duanjia Archway and East Xiaoshunmen in this city was previously decided by the Provincial Government to be widened to facilitate traffic. A notice was issued to the residents in the area to comply with the designated boundaries, demolish and retreat their houses, and complete the demolition and retreat by September 25 in order to start construction. It is learned that the residents in the area have complied with the designated boundaries and completed the demolition and retreat. Construction will begin within days.

Jiading: Land Tax Penalty Extension for Half a Month

The first installment of land price tax for the 25th year in this county was levied from August 15th to the 14th of this month, a period of two months. Regulations stipulate that a late payment penalty should be levied for exceeding the deadline. County Chief Guo, considering that the number of collections within the deadline was small, extended the penalty period by half a month to show compassion for the people. Approval has been obtained and a notice has been issued to inform the public.

Huangdu: Robbery of Farmhouses

On the night of the 19th, eight bandits, speaking in Hakka dialect and holding electric torches and pistols, broke into the home of farmer Liu Guiquan near Huangdu Town in the Second District. Two people stood guard outside, and the rest entered the room to rob. They left after a while. After checking the losses, it was estimated that jewelry, clothing, cloth, chickens, ducks, and other items worth a total of 100 yuan in legal currency were taken.

Fengxian: Request to Reduce Fares at the Minhang Ferry

Yesterday, on the Fengxian Pubei section, which is the opposite shore of Minhang, the ferry sank into the Pu River due to carrying too many passengers, resulting in the deaths of more than 30 ferry passengers. Seeing this, Diao Yebai and other people from all walks of life in the county specially petitioned the Construction Department to ban old ferries and request Minhang Ferry to reduce fares so that farmers can safely take the ferry, so as not to greedily seek cheapness and cause accidents.

Wuxi: Strike Wave Subsides

Shops in the area near Yinglong Town shed outside the West Gate of this county were agitated by a dispute over market scales and canal scales over a purchase of one yuan of fresh crabs by the cook of the Yinglong Orange Police Station of the Fourth Public Security Bureau at the Yan Yun Ji fish shop, arousing public anger and causing a strike. It is learned that after this incident occurred, the town chief of the area, Chen Nianzu, and the district chief of the First District, Qian Zhongliang, reported to the Public Security Bureau. Director Zhang met them and promised to find a way to mediate. He immediately ordered inspectors Chen Hoyu and Patrol Officer Tong to go to persuade them to resume business. At the same time, he placed the cook Yin Ada under surveillance and sent him to the headquarters for interrogation. At the same time, Zhang ordered the Fourth Bureau to release Xu Dequan, the bookkeeper of Yan Yun Ji, the employees Qin Ating and Chen Asan, and the bystander Shen Ating, who were detained that night. The matter was settled. On the morning of the 24th, the striking shops in the area all opened for business and resumed normal operations.

Breaking Up a Morphine Den

Public Security Bureau Director Zhang Da received a secret report yesterday stating that there was a private morphine injection den in a dilapidated house next to the Zhuang Ding team at No. 10 Jia, West Street, Qianzhou Town, Ninth District, and requested that the police be dispatched to arrest them. After receiving the report, Zhang immediately ordered Inspector Gu Jiafeng to lead the police to search the countryside. Upon arriving at the destination, they saw Tang Sanbao, Bian Caigen, and Tang Wenqi all injecting morphine, so they were all arrested. A morphine needle was seized from Tang Sanbao's hand, and a small package of morphine was found under a broken mat. They were immediately taken to the bureau and transferred to the county government for transfer to the Second District Security Command for interrogation.

Changshu: Red Cross Malaria Eradication Team Departs

In the Fifth and Sixth Districts here, malignant malaria has been prevalent recently, and deaths have followed one after another. Farmers have shallow knowledge and often rely on superstitious worship of ghosts and gods instead of fundamental treatment, which has led to extremely rapid spread. In view of this, the Red Cross Society has specially joined forces with the Western Medical Association to organize a malaria eradication team, with the Red Cross responsible for economic medicines and the physicians responsible for treatment. The first team has already departed, with doctors Zhou Tianlai, Yu Jishi, Shao Yufan, Huang Chengxi, and Zhu Bingwen appointed to be responsible for diagnosis, and Red Cross staff members Shi Shouzhi, Huang Tongwei, and Chen Xiaomei also sent to assist. They went to Zhitang, Xijiashi, and Lao Wushi on the 24th, and are expected to return to the city in three days, after which a second team will be sent.

County Government Urges Grain Tax Collection

The county government has now begun to collect the first installment of field tax for the 25th year, but more than ten days after the start of the collection, the amount collected is zero. The reasons for this are nothing more than the serious situation, the proliferation of rumors, and the fact that those who do not understand the situation are watching each other. However, the county government needs a large amount of funds at this time. If the taxes are not collected, how can it be maintained? On the 23rd, it summoned all businesses in the urban area and ordered them to pay within a limited time. At the same time, grain cabinet staff members Zhu Zhenxia, Song Aizhi, Gu Yansheng, Zhou Quan, and Shi Jiagan were dispatched to various rural areas to collect taxes from the rural businesses within a limited time to meet urgent needs.

Hangzhou: Petition to Reduce the Amount of Grain Storage

The Zhejiang Provincial Federation of Chambers of Commerce believes that the grain storage allocation standards in this province are too burdensome for merchants. They have repeatedly received telegrams from more than 20 counties, including Quxian, Wukang, Jinhua, Jiaxing, Yiwu, Jiashan, Tongxiang, Shangyu, Shaoxing, and Lanxi, requesting relief. After being transferred to the provincial government, they were disapproved. The Joint Meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees decided to publicly elect Chairman Jin Runquan, Committee Members Xie Hucheng, Zhou Yangsong, Lu Chujue, Chen Qinshi, and Xu Xinggong, and eight others as representatives to visit Xu Qingfu of the Civil Affairs Department at 11:00 AM on the 24th to report everything and request a slight change. Xu met them personally, and the result was quite satisfactory.

Hangzhou-Shan Road Station Opens for Business

The entire line of the Hangzhou-Shan Road, including the road surface and bridges, has been completed and has been submitted to the Construction Department for inspection. As for the location of stations along the route, the Operations Section Chief of the First District Management Office has conducted an inspection and decided to set up 11 stations: Hangzhou, Qingtai Dou, Qibao, Qiaosi, Linping, Chongde, Xiangxiang, Puyuan, Jiaxing, Jiashan, and Fengjing. In the future, it is planned to run a direct bus once a day between Hangzhou and Fengjing, and a local bus once each between Chonghang and Chongjia. Because the inspection still requires considerable procedures and the bridges also need to be repaired, it will not be possible to open for business until November 10.

Nantong: Epidemic Trend in Tongru Declines

Malignant malaria in Nantong and Rugao counties has spread over a wide area. After diagnosis and treatment by the epidemic prevention team, it has recently shown a peaceful state and fewer deaths. The epidemic prevention team has divided the epidemic area into several units, and each team of doctors is diagnosing and injecting in turn according to the Baojia households every day. After each township is completed, the mountain township chief inspects each household to completely eliminate the epidemic. Within a week, the epidemic can be completely eliminated.

Letter Received

To the Esteemed Editor: We have just read the news in your newspaper on the 21st of this month, "Smuggling Ronin Cause Disturbance at Jinan Station," which stated that customs officials "evaded in advance," "fled empty-handed," and that "Director Lin Lemin also avoided and dared not go to the station," etc., which differs slightly from the facts. On the afternoon of the 18th, at 4:30 PM, five customs officers from our office, along with police officers, seized two cars of smuggled goods at Luokou National Bridge and transported the smuggled goods back to the Jinpu Freight Yard in order to transport them to Beijing. At the same time, the smuggling ronin were handed over to the police officers at the yard for handling. Unexpectedly, at about 6:00 PM, when inspector Liu Maoyun, who was on the night shift, was working, more than 100 ronin suddenly gathered, armed with weapons, and rushed to the office, forcing them to hand over the seized goods. Inspector Liu politely reasoned with them, but the ronin did not allow any explanation and violently beat him, causing him to faint and lose consciousness. They also sent people to monitor him. After receiving the report, our director immediately rushed to the Public Security Bureau and sent people to the military and police agencies for assistance, but no effective assistance was obtained. At the same time, dozens of ronin took five cars to our residence at the China Travel Service guest house and violently beat customs officers Gao Zongqi and Zhang Jiakun, then forcibly dragged them to Jinpu Station and forced them to return the seized goods, stating that they would not release them unless the seized goods were returned. The three beaten customs officers, along with our director, were trying to negotiate with the military, police, and Japanese consular police, but the smuggling ronin were unreasonable and insisted on returning the seized goods. Then, the Inspector Li of the Public Security Bureau strongly advised them to avoid escalating the situation and to rescue the three beaten customs officers. They had no choice but to temporarily agree to hand over the seized goods to the Japanese Consulate for safekeeping, and the Japanese Consulate issued an official receipt. The above is a rough situation. We are deeply afraid that the outside world will not understand the truth and will not forgive us. Therefore, we specially write this letter to correct the record. We hope that you will publish it. Sincerely, Jinan Inspection Office for Preventing Smuggling on the Road, Customs. October 23rd.

To the Esteemed Editor: The news about the Changshu Prison published in your newspaper on October 15th contains many inaccuracies. In the past, our prison seemed to be slightly lax in its management, such as allowing prisoners to arbitrarily drink alcohol and smoke. After the new warden Gong took office, he immediately rectified and prohibited these bad habits. At the same time, several thieves violated the rules, and for prevention, they were all shackled, which caused resentment. During breakfast on the——3rd, several thieves restricted the food intake of the majority. After the warden advised them, the turmoil subsided immediately. It lasted only a few minutes, and there was no reduction in food rations as reported. We are writing this letter to state the facts and ask that you publish it in the "Letters to the Editor" column to clarify the truth. Sincerely, Changshu County Prison. October 19th.

Local News

Shanghai Celebrates with Flag-Raising: All Circles Present Airplanes as Birthday Gifts; Naming Ceremony Held Yesterday; Mayor Wu Led the Ceremony; Airplane Performance Concluded with Flight to Hangzhou; 150,000 Spectators

Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, the "Zhongzheng Team" airplane naming ceremony, organized by the committee commemorating Chairman Chiang's 50th birthday and funded by donations from all sectors of the city to present airplanes to the government, took place at the Longhua Airport. Numerous representatives from various groups attended. Mayor Wu and others delivered speeches, and after the naming ceremony, air force pilots performed demonstrations. Approximately 150,000 people from Shanghai flocked to watch, and the entire city celebrated by raising flags. The unprecedented enthusiasm is recorded below.

On Longhua Road

The autumn sky was high and clear, with a gentle and warm breeze. Yesterday afternoon, Longhua Road was almost entirely enveloped in an atmosphere of excitement. The fervent enthusiasm of the entire citizenry towards aviation was evident on the face of every citizen. From Jingji Road, across Jingji Bridge, and all the way to the airport, spanning over ten li, Longhua Station was filled with people from 12:00 PM, braving the journey and walking to participate in the airplane presentation and birthday celebration naming ceremony. People rubbed shoulders and bumped elbows. Cars, bicycles, and rickshaws were connected and winding together, losing their ability to speed. Armed police officers tasked with maintaining traffic safety exhausted their abilities, carefully managing the various vehicles and strictly enforcing traffic regulations. Along the road, national flags were hung in front of every residence, shadowed by green trees, creating a unique atmosphere. Public buses traveling between Ximen and Longhua, and special trains running from the South Station to Longhua, were filled to the brim on every trip. By 2:00 PM, the roads became even more congested. The traffic at Tianyao Bridge was completely blocked. Even Mayor Wu's vehicle could not move forward, so he and his wife got out of the car and walked. The crowd at the airport only began to disperse at 7:00 PM, truly an unprecedented spectacle.

A Glimpse of the Venue

The main entrance of the venue was decorated with a tall, colorful archway made of pine and cypress. Party and national flags were placed on the left and right sides, and a red silk banner with gold characters reading "Shanghai City Airplane Presentation and Birthday Celebration Naming Ceremony" was hung in the middle. The venue was surrounded by iron fences. The entrance to the special ticket area was in front of the Eurasia Company office, and the entrance to the general ticket area was in front of the Cement Factory Road. Both entrances had registration books, and personnel from the airplane presentation committee collected tickets. The standing areas for special and general ticket holders were separated by red and green cloth. A platform facing south was set up in the center of the venue, surrounded by red cloth, with a red silk banner hanging above. In the middle of the platform hung a portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and a photograph of Chairman Chiang. Ten airplanes were parked in a line on the empty space in front of the platform. The nose of each plane was covered with a party and national flag. Pilots stood on both sides of each plane. The planes were surrounded by ropes, guarded by security police, to prevent spectators from approaching. Inside and outside the venue, public security bureau police officers, security team police officers, and Boy Scouts from the Boy Scout Council maintained order. Although there were many people, order was maintained because all areas were separated by red and green cloth. Loudspeakers were set up in the venue to broadcast speeches.

Ten Airplanes Fly to Shanghai

The ten fighter planes purchased by Shanghai arrived in Shanghai at the beginning of this month. However, due to the lack of a suitable airport, they flew to Hangzhou and landed at the aviation school. Yesterday, to attend the naming ceremony, the planes took off in formation from Hangzhou at 10:00 AM and arrived in Shanghai at noon. They landed at Longhua Airport to await the naming ceremony.

Attending Representatives

Among those present yesterday were Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Central Committee member Chu Minyi, Vice President of the Judicial Yuan Tan Zhen, President of Jiaotong University Li Zhaohuan, Songhu Garrison Commander Yang Hu, Aviation Commission representative Huang Bingheng, Public Security Bureau Chief Cai Jingjun, Pan Gongzhan, Xu Peihuang, and representatives from various groups, including Lin Kanghou, Wang Xiaolai, Zhou Xuexiang, Yu Qiaqing, Zhao Jinqing, Sun Qiuping, Yao Xijiu, Huang Zhaoxiong, Xie Zhongfu, Zhu Zigao, Tong Xingbai, Zhang Shouyong, Bei Songsun, Zhang Xiaolin, Mao Heyuan, and Gu Xinyi. The presidium consisted of fifteen people: Wu Tiecheng, Cai Jingjun, Yang Hu, Song Xilian, Zhang Shouyong, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, Zhu Zigao, Sun Qiuping, Gu Xinyi, Huang Zhaoxiong, Li Zicai, and Tong Xingbai. Mayor Wu presided over the ceremony, which included: (1) playing music, (2) singing the Party anthem, (3) paying the highest respect to the Party and national flag and the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, (4) the chairman reverently reading Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will, (5) the chairman delivering an opening address, (6) speeches, and (7) holding the naming ceremony and aerial performance.

Mayor's Speech

Mayor Wu, as chairman, first gave a speech, saying, "Members of the presidium, citizens, more than 100,000 people from Shanghai are gathered here today to attend the airplane presentation and naming ceremony, an unprecedented event for the city of Shanghai, demonstrating the respect and sincerity of the 3.5 million citizens of Shanghai towards our leader. The ten airplanes presented as birthday gifts are named: Shanghai Municipal Government, Shanghai Party Headquarters, Shanghai Police, Shanghai Business, Shanghai Anti-Smoking, Shanghai Ningbo, Shanghai Training Students, Shanghai Tourism, Shanghai Grains, and Shanghai Xiangchengyi, forming the Zhongzheng Team. After the naming ceremony, the Zhongzheng Team will fly to the capital, carrying the respect and enthusiasm of all the citizens of Shanghai to celebrate Chairman Chiang's 50th birthday. Chairman Chiang completed the great task of the National Revolution and unification, laying the foundation for China's prosperity and strength. The people should respect and honor meritorious deeds, expressing a unified respect and enthusiasm nationwide. In these extremely difficult times, the citizens of Shanghai can still enthusiastically donate money to purchase airplanes to celebrate birthdays, strengthen national defense, and advocate patriotism and love for the leader nationwide. This unprecedented and fervent expression undoubtedly demonstrates the determination of Shanghai's 3.5 million citizens to concentrate all their efforts to support the leader, overcome national difficulties, revive the nation, and build a new China to establish itself in the world today. Without national defense, there is no way to maintain the survival of the nation and people. If China has no national defense, or its national defense is insufficient, its nation and people are in danger of extinction. The air force is the greatest power of national defense. In China today, to build national defense, it is especially necessary to strengthen the air force. National defense must concentrate the spiritual and material strength of the entire nation to build and strengthen it. Therefore, national construction, such as education, industry, agriculture, and mining, must be centered on national defense. Only in this way will its construction be nationalistic, and only nationalistic construction can maintain the nation's survival. Therefore, China's construction today is nationalistic construction, and China's national defense today is defensive national defense. China's self-defense is to seek China's security, maintain peace in East Asia, and protect world peace. These are the highest responsibilities and obligations of mankind, which the Chinese people should thoroughly recognize and make positive contributions to the security of China and the peace of East Asia and the world. The significance of today's airplane presentation and birthday celebration lies in this."

Huang Bingheng's Speech

I am very honored to participate on behalf of the Aviation Commission. This nationwide campaign of purchasing airplanes and donating money demonstrates the people's fervent admiration for the national leader. Chairman Chiang has been working hard for the people and the country since he set out from Guangzhou ten years ago, which is admired by the people. Now that Chairman Chiang is celebrating his 50th birthday and the country is unified, I hope he will lead the people to use the power of unity to strive for construction, abolish unequal treaties, and embark on the road to revival. Wang Xiaolai's Speech

Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, said, "This year is the 25th year of the Republic of China, and also Chairman Chiang's 50th birthday. The date falls on the third week after National Day, which is a sign that his birth is not accidental. Considering the ancient tradition of celebrating centenarian birthdays, the age of fifty is like the 'sun at its zenith,' and it can also symbolize that although the country is in difficult and troubled times, with this great pillar supporting the central government, the country's fate will surely advance without end. People from all walks of life across the country, in order to express their gratitude to Chairman Chiang for his tireless efforts, have donated money to purchase airplanes to present to the government to commemorate Chairman Chiang's 50th birthday. The airplanes purchased with the funds collected in this city are numbered as ten. Today, we are holding a naming ceremony. As a citizen and as a member of the organizing committee for purchasing airplanes to celebrate birthdays, I cannot remain silent. I would like to say a word to the citizens of the entire city. In the past, the State of Lu in the Spring and Autumn Period was a weak country, often bullied by Qi and Chu. The 'Bi Gong' chapter of the 'Lu Song' was written to celebrate Duke Xi of Lu's birthday. The reason for celebrating Duke Xi was that they said, 'May you live ten thousand years, may your longevity be without end.' The reason for celebrating the State of Lu was that they said, 'If Jing and Shu are punished, then no one will dare to accept us.' In modern terms, it means that foreigners dare not bully us. It can be seen that a country must reach a point where foreigners dare not bully it before it can encounter a birthday celebration and raise a glass in celebration. However, the people of Lu at that time used 'a thousand chariots of state and thirty thousand soldiers' to celebrate Duke Xi and the State of Lu. Chariots are war chariots, and soldiers are soldiers. Only when the people can use war chariots and soldiers to celebrate the country can they achieve a situation where the State of Lu, although weak, can survive. Our purchase of airplanes to celebrate birthdays today has the same goal as the 'Lu Song.' Therefore, to achieve the same goal as the 'Lu Song,' taking 'a thousand chariots of state and thirty thousand soldiers' as an example, there should be at least a thousand airplanes and thirty thousand pilots. The current stage we have reached is still far from the intended goal. Currently, there is an initiative in this city's newspapers to launch a 'contribute to the country for one day' campaign. The members of the Chamber of Commerce have first decided to actively promote it. I, in my capacity as Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, formally propose that all sectors strive to promote this national salvation 'one day' campaign. If farmers, industrialists, merchants, and students across the country can use one day's income to purchase airplanes and celebrate birthdays, I hope that compatriots across the country will rise up and not neglect this 'one day,' and gather the strength of 450 million people to establish the national foundation of the Republic of China for billions of years. Let us start this endeavor today."

Speeches from All Sides

Songhu Garrison Commander Yang Hu said, "Chairman Chiang is the leader of the Party and the country. His life's efforts have been entirely for the Party and the country. Therefore, presenting airplanes to Chairman Chiang is presenting them to the Party and the country." Training Commander Song Xilian said, "Among the ten airplanes, there is a Training Team, which was donated by the city's training students. Of the hundreds of thousands of students in the city, only the training students have this expression, because they have a complete organization." Tong Xingbai of the Municipal Party Headquarters said, "When Chairman Chiang celebrates his birthday, the people of the country celebrate in two ways: materially and spiritually. Chairman Chiang is the leader of the country, and his responsibility is to defend the country. Therefore, the best material gift is airplanes, which can strengthen national defense. As for the spiritual aspect, I hope that the people of the country will fully contribute their talents and spirits and work together to save the country." Mayor Wu then reported that the Catholic Church in China had also donated 50,000 yuan under the order of the Archbishop to present airplanes as birthday gifts. Lu Bohong then said, "The Catholic Church in China, under the order of the Pope's representative, has donated 50,000 yuan to purchase two ambulance planes to contribute to the government, to express the gratitude of the nation's 3.5 million Catholics to the national leader."

Naming Ceremony Ritual

After the speeches, Mayor Wu and his wife, and the representatives who named each airplane, stepped off the ceremony platform and marched to the venue led by the military band to conduct the naming ceremony. 1. Shanghai Municipal Government: Mayor Wu and his wife. 2. Shanghai Party Headquarters: Tong Xingbai and his wife. 3. Shanghai Anti-Smoking: Du Yuesheng and his wife. 4. Shanghai Business: Wang Xiaolai and his wife. 5. Shanghai Police: Cai Jingjun and his wife. 6. Shanghai Tourism: Sun Qiuping and his wife. 7. Shanghai Ningbo: Yu Qiaqing and Mao Heyuan's wife. 8. Shanghai Training: Song Xilian and his wife. 9. Shanghai Grains: Gu Xinyi and his daughter. 10. Shanghai Xiangchengyi: Zhu Zigao and his wife. After the representatives who named each airplane took a group photo in front of the airplane, the party and national flag emblem covering the airplane's nose was removed amidst the sound of music, marking the completion of the ceremony. The engines were started in preparation for the aerial performance.

Aerial Performance

The Zhongzheng Team planes were flown by team leader Li Dan, deputy team leader Liu Zhihan, and team members Fan Jinhan, Gong Yeyi, Liu Zhesheng, Tan Wen, Wang Kai, Zhang Xiaoliang, Wang Yuanbo, and Liu Shufan. All the pilots were dressed in air force uniforms and stood by their planes. After the naming ceremony, they got into their planes, started the engines, and planes one through nine, led by team leader Li, passed in front of the classic ceremony platform, circled to the west of the venue, and sped southeast, taking off into the air. After circling the venue once, they formed three small teams, with one team in the lead and two teams following on the left and right rear, flying low over the venue. Then, the nine planes formed a character "人" (person) and flew high overhead. Later, they formed the character "一" (one) and flew forward in a straight line. When they reached the airspace above the venue, they rolled to one side and descended, forming a ring and flying several circles, then flying low over the ground one by one. Their movements were agile and their order was impeccable. As for plane number ten, flown by Liu Zhihan, it performed independently: 1. Continuous somersaults, 2. Continuous slow rolls, fast rolls, 3. British hat slow turns, 4. Inverted flight, 5. Ascending slow rolls, 6. Wingover, 7. Dive, etc. The high level of skill impressed the audience. At about 4:00 PM, the planes formed a team and flew south back to Hangzhou, planning to fly to Beijing on the 31st to participate in the birthday celebration and airplane presentation. Various groups in this city will send representatives to attend.

Another Performance

In order to promote interest in civil aviation, the organizers specially invited female aviator Li Xiaqing to perform at the venue before the naming ceremony. Yesterday, the lady wore a white canvas flight suit and circulated among the guests, with elegant demeanor, which attracted much attention. Before the ceremony, the sound of an engine was heard, and a yellow-winged "Fleet" training aircraft took off to perform, landing only after about a quarter of an hour. The plane was piloted by Zhang Shouchun, a member of the China Flying Club, and instructor Chen Xiayun. The altitude reached more than 2,400 feet. Zhang is a graduate of the Hong Kong Aviation School. Then, Ms. Li and instructor Yang Zhaofan flew another aircraft of the same type, ascending and flying low, circling the venue several times and performing techniques such as inverted flight and somersaults, which were quite impressive. After getting out of the plane, the lady went to the ceremony platform to participate in the ceremony.

Total Number of Airplanes Presented

The Central Aviation Commission specially sent Huang Bingheng to Shanghai to participate in the naming of the Zhongzheng Team airplanes in Shanghai. Mr. Huang returned to Beijing last night after attending the ceremony. A reporter from the New Sound News Agency interviewed Mr. Huang yesterday. According to him, the total number of airplanes obtained from the provinces and cities that launched the campaign to purchase airplanes to celebrate Chairman Chiang's 50th birthday is more than sixty. The central government has notified them separately to fly the presented airplanes to Beijing on the 29th to prepare for the grand presentation ceremony on the 31st.

Representatives from All Walks of Life To Hold Public Memorial Ceremony for the Late Chairman Hu This Morning; At 9:00 AM at the Grand Auditorium of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; The City Will Lower Flags to Half-Mast and Suspend Entertainment in Mourning

Today (the 25th) is the date of the national funeral ceremony for the late Chairman Hu ZhanTang of the Central Executive Committee. In addition to sending representatives to Guangzhou to attend the burial ceremony, the party and government circles of this city have decided to hold a public memorial ceremony at 9:00 AM this morning at the Grand Auditorium of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at Tianhougong Bridge. All sectors of the city will lower flags to half-mast and suspend entertainment for one day to express mourning. The details are as follows:

Staff: Presiding celebrant: Mayor Wu Tiecheng; Assisting celebrants: Tao Baichuan and Tong Xingbai, Standing Committee members of the Municipal Party Headquarters Executive Committee; Eulogy reader: Zhu Manyun; Master of ceremonies: Zhang Hanyun; Recorder: She Mengsen; Reception: Li Dachao, Zhou Guoping, Chen Bisheng, and twelve others; Ushers: Zhang Yunceng, Huang Xianggu, Huang E, Li Baiqing, Wu Xianren, Xia Weiqing, Yang Dean, Ren Bin, Yu Yaoqiu, Tong Muge, Zhu Xiaochun, Wu Di, and twelve others. The Municipal Public Security Bureau will send a military band to participate in playing music and police to maintain order.

Ceremony: (1) All stand at attention; (2) Play mourning music; (3) Presiding celebrant takes position; (4) Assisting celebrants take position; (5) Sing the Party anthem; (6) Bow three times to the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and the portrait of the late Chairman Hu; (7) Chairman respectfully reads Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will; (8) Three minutes of silence; (9) Present flowers; (10) Read the eulogy; (11) Play mourning music; (12) Ceremony concludes.

Eulogy: "On this, the 25th day of October in the 25th year of the Republic of China, the date of the national funeral of the late Chairman Hu Gong Zhantang, the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive and Supervisory Committees of the Kuomintang of China, and the Shanghai Municipal Government, leading all party members and the public, respectfully present flowers and offer this eulogy: Heaven is unkind, taking away our great man. A star falls in Guangdong, and the sun and moon lose their light. The Party loses its defender, and the country loses its pillar. All of us Chinese people are filled with grief, raising our heads to the south and shedding tears on our clothes. The national crisis is deepening, and the whole country is alarmed. Internal stability and external resistance, resisting aggression and saving the country, expanding our influence and straightening out our affairs, all depend on virtuous and capable people. In one sudden death, who will correct the discipline? Now, on the occasion of the national funeral, the ceremony is magnificent, the tomb is lush, and the cemetery trees are verdant. The tomb is high, and the tombstone stands on the Dragon Hill. Burying loyalty in the Guangdong Mountains, it will be passed down for eternity. Peace and tranquility have been achieved, and the legacy will be long. It will be immortal for centuries, forever preserving the boundless. Alas, may you rest in peace!"

Anti-Tuberculosis Association Held Its Annual Meeting Yesterday, Approving Various Reports and Re-electing Directors and Supervisors

The Chinese Anti-Tuberculosis Association held its annual meeting yesterday at 3:30 PM on the ninth floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA, reporting on association affairs and re-electing directors and supervisors. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM. Details are as follows:

Attending Representatives

Those present yesterday included Mayor Wu (represented by Li Ting'an), Li Ting'an, Pan Gongzhan (represented by Hu Shuyi), Cai Jingjun (represented by Chen Changqing), Gan Xiaolai (represented by Shi Menglan), Ji Zhangjian (represented by Du Hesheng), Wu Yun Chu (represented by Fang Zhicheng), Lei Kenan representing the Social Bureau, Zhu Jiarang representing the New Life Movement, Liu Wenlin representing the Child Welfare Association, members Yan Fuqing, Yuan Haiping, Xu Xinru, Cao Yongzheng, Yang Hao, and over a hundred others.

Chairman's Address

After formal greetings, Chairman Wu Tiecheng, represented by Li Ting'an, delivered an address, briefly stating: "The harm caused by tuberculosis is most alarming. Every year, over a hundred thousand people in our country die from tuberculosis, and more than ten million are bedridden due to the disease. There are also tens of millions of others who have not been properly surveyed. Suffering from this disease leads to physical weakness and mental depression. We firmly believe that if we want to revive our nation, we must pay attention to the health of the people. Given the circumstances of our nation, tuberculosis prevention is an essential task for realizing public health. Although our association is dedicated to tuberculosis prevention, its real mission is to promote the health of the nation. We now have this organization in Shanghai, and we will expand it to the whole country in the future. Especially during this critical period of national crisis, when the entire nation is united and striving for national revival, we should pay more attention and make greater efforts in important work related to national health, such as tuberculosis prevention."

Representatives' Addresses

Subsequently, Pan Gongzhan, representing Hu Shuyi, delivered an address, briefly stating: "Tuberculosis prevention is an important task for promoting national health. Efforts to prevent tuberculosis can be considered from two aspects: First, in terms of knowledge, to make everyone aware of the dangers of tuberculosis and the importance of its prevention. Second, in terms of habits, to help everyone develop good hygienic practices, such as spitting and dietary habits, which will yield significant results. The flourishing of industry and commerce and the growth of population in this city make tuberculosis prevention particularly important. Recognizing the alarming spread of tuberculosis in urban areas, we have established this organization. In the future, the education, commercial, industrial, and social bureau sectors are willing to cooperate to promote tuberculosis prevention." Cai Jingjun, representing Chen Changqing, delivered an address, briefly stating: "Our country is regarded by the world as the 'Sick Man of East Asia.' Although enlightened people and government authorities have been promoting hygiene, many ignorant people are still mired in superstition, which has not yielded great results. Therefore, we should focus on breaking down superstitions and promoting proper scientific hygiene methods. Tuberculosis is a serious threat to our nation, and your association's dedication to tuberculosis prevention is truly saving the nation." Ding Huikang also gave a speech, which is omitted here.

Three-Year Plan

After reports from various working committees, Yan Fuqing reported on future work plans, briefly stating: "Our association has been established for three years, and most of our past work has focused on promotion. In the future, we should focus on the implementation of practical work. This practical work should start with projects that meet the needs of the majority of people and provide the most benefits. We often see that diseases such as cholera and leprosy, due to their ease of transmission, lead to general attention to prevention. However, the transmission of tuberculosis is even easier than that of cholera and leprosy. Whether in the milk of humans, cattle, or sheep, or in other foods and in the air, it is very easy to transmit. Recent doctor's surveys show that 80 to 90 percent of children aged from birth to twelve have the disease's root. Sometimes, because the body is relatively healthy, it is not discovered. However, if the body is slightly out of balance or not properly protected, the symptoms of the disease can appear. Although our association is limited by funding, I plan to focus on the following projects in the next three years, selecting those that are more economical and more important: (1) Children's health camp. This project requires limited time and less funding, and its benefits to children are significant. (2) Establish two new clinics each year, with an expected total of six in three years. Those who are not ill or only mildly ill will be examined. Tuberculosis in the second or third stage not only costs a lot of money, but it is also difficult to cure. (3) Establish sanatoriums. The city's sanatoriums have only 350 beds, but in reality, 3,500 are not enough. Nine-tenths of tuberculosis patients cannot get proper care. Although setting up sanatoriums is costly, it will depend on future financial capabilities."

Improve Dining

Then, a proposal was discussed. Peng Wenying proposed a discussion on the method of improving dining habits. The reason is that the original Chinese dining method, where everyone uses chopsticks and spoons to take food from the same bowl, is more dangerous than spitting if someone at the table has tuberculosis. The proposed method is to organize a research association to improve dining habits and request the authorities to renovate public dining places in accordance with the law. It was unanimously approved and referred to the next board of directors for implementation.

Re-election of Directors and Supervisors

Finally, directors and supervisors were re-elected. The list is as follows: (Directors) Wu Tiecheng, Lu Bohong, Li Ting'an, Yan Fuqing, Weng Zhilong, Pan Gongzhan, Chen Heqin, Wang Xiaoying, J.H. Jordan, Liu Hongsheng, Li Fuzhuo, Lu Ganchen, Huang Renzhi, Lin Kanghou, Gu Yuqi, Zhu Qinglan, Wu Yunchu, Li Denghui, Guo Shun, Xu Jianping, Xu Shiying, Dong Xianguang, Hu Yunqiu, Li Zuwei, Jin Shuchu, Lu Yongchun, Feng Shaoshan, Diao Xinde, Chen Zhifang, Li Dachao, Tan Shixin, Hu Guanming, Song Guobin, Qian Muhan, Cai Jingjun, Zhu Shaoping, Yu Zuoting, Liang Xiaochu, Cai Xiangsun, J. Rabaute, Liu Rui'en, S.M. Garnn, Zhang Zhijiang, Chu Minyi, Xiang Longxun, Chen Guangfu, Zhao Jinqing, Wu Liande, Mrs. Xiao Zhiji, Zhu Hengbi, Zhou Bangjun, Liu Wang Liming, Ouyang Huichong. (Standing Directors) Lu Bohong, Li Ting'an, Yan Fuqing, Weng Zhilong, Huang Zifang, Chen Heqin, Wu Tiecheng, Joel Ten, Pan Gongzhan, Wang Xiaoying, Shi Enming. (Supervisors) Du Yuesheng, Pang Jingzhou, Ding Fubao, Qian Xinzhi, Yao Mulian, Liu Zhanen, Yu Qiaqing.

Ambassador Jiang Departed Yesterday Morning for His New Post in the Soviet Union, Offering Parting Words to Uphold Unity and Avoid Reckless Concessions

Dr. Jiang Tingfu, the newly appointed ambassador to the Soviet Union, departed yesterday morning at 8:00 AM, accompanied by his wife and two sons, as well as Shi Zhaoying, the newly appointed first secretary of the embassy; Yuan Daofeng and his wife, the second secretary; Geng Kuang, the third secretary; Li Nenggeng and his wife, assistants; Xi Men Zonghua, director; and over a dozen servants, aboard the Soviet Russian Assistance Association's "Northern" ship for his new post.

Special Ship to Cross the Huangpu River

Ambassador Jiang and his wife left the International Hotel at 6:30 AM and, at around 7:00 AM, boarded the specially prepared customs ship "Jinghui" from the Xin Guan wharf to the Yitaixing wharf in Pudong to board the "Northern" ship. Secretary Shi Zhaoying and others had taken the Soviet Russian Assistance Association's ferry to Pudong at 6:30 AM. The ship set sail from Shanghai at 8:00 AM sharp, expected to arrive in Vladivostok in 29 days, where they will transfer to the Siberian Railway train to proceed directly to Moscow to take up their new posts. The ship was originally scheduled to depart in the afternoon, but was advanced due to Ambassador Jiang's need to make the journey.

Farewells from All Sides

Mayor Wu Tiecheng, the newly appointed ambassador to the United States, Wang Zhengting, Customs Director Zheng Lai, Director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Office in Shanghai, Zhou Jue, former Director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Office in Shanghai, Tang Nianci, and Liu Zhanen, Zou Bingwen, Wang Zhixin, and Soviet Ambassador to China Bogomolov, who traveled from Beijing especially, led the Soviet Consul General in Shanghai, Spielberg, Military Attaché Repin, First Secretary Melad, Second Secretary Saratov Zhifu, and over 30 friends and relatives of the Jiang family, to the wharf to say goodbye. Mayor Wu and his wife, Ambassador Wang and his wife, Soviet Ambassador Bogomolov and his wife, presented Ambassador Jiang and his wife with many baskets of flowers in remembrance.

Parting Words

Before departing, Ambassador Jiang gave a parting message to the nation, saying, "As I depart, I have only two words to say to the people of the country: first, internally, uphold unity; second, externally, do not make reckless concessions. If we can do this, the country will have a way out. This is what I hope for most." He also said that after leaving Shanghai, he plans to arrive in Moscow by the 7th of next month to attend the Soviet National Day celebration. It is also reported that Wu Nanru, the current counselor of the embassy in the Soviet Union, has been abroad for more than two years. According to the regulations of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, after Ambassador Jiang takes office, he will be relieved of his duties as acting ambassador after two months and will request leave to return to the country.

Records of Contemporary Figures' Movements

Zhang Jia'ao and Zou Lin arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning by train from Beijing.

Wang Boqun, Chu Minyi, and Fu Rulin took the overnight train to Beijing yesterday.

Kita left Beijing yesterday afternoon by express train and arrived in Shanghai at 10:50 PM last night.

The French Ambassador to China, Nagear, has returned to Peiping from Beijing and arrived in Shanghai yesterday.

Sino-US Full-Line Trial Flight Successful, Crossing the Pacific Ocean for Over 10,000 Miles, Arriving in Longhua at 5 PM Yesterday, Carrying Seven Passengers in Total, Five Americans and Two Filipinos.

Following British approval of China-America's establishment of a station in Hong Kong, the first trial flight of a direct China-America flight arrived in Longhua at 5:00 PM yesterday from Hong Kong, carrying seven people who departed from the United States, including the General Manager of Pan-Pacific Airlines, Trippe, and the Chairman of the Board, Whituery. Trippe and others are the first to arrive in China directly from the United States via commercial airlines. Regular joint flights between China National Aviation Corporation (CNAC) and Pan-Pacific Airlines will begin next month. A reporter from the Shenzhou News Agency provides the following details:

Completion of the China-America Route

With the approval from the British side for the establishment of a station in Hong Kong, the China-America air route will soon be fully operational. Trippe, the General Manager of Pan-Pacific Airlines, Whituery, the Chairman of the Board, and Best, the company's Far East Manager, departed from the United States this month aboard the "Clipper" aircraft. They arrived in the Philippines some days ago, and after obtaining permission from the Hong Kong authorities via telegram, departed from the Philippines to Hong Kong via Macau the day before. Trippe and his party then took the "Fujian" and "Guangdong" aircraft from Hong Kong yesterday morning at 8:30 AM and 9:00 AM, respectively, to Shanghai, completing the full China-America flight.

Arrival of Two Managers in Shanghai

After departing from Hong Kong, Howard, the Far East Manager of the Associated Press, and McGatto, the Manila Manager of Pan-Pacific Airlines, arrived in Shanghai at 4:15 PM aboard the "Fujian" aircraft. Trippe and his wife, the General Manager of Pan-Pacific Airlines, Whituery, the Chairman of the Board, and Best and his wife, the Far East Manager of Pan-Pacific Airlines, arrived in Shanghai at 5:00 PM aboard the "Guangdong" aircraft. Those who came to welcome them included Huang Jiangquan, Chairman of China National Aviation Corporation, Dai Enji, General Manager, Ericsson, Chief Engineer, Nie Kaiyi, Deputy Director of the Flight Group, and Huang Baoxian, Director of the Business Group, among others.

Passengers Flying Across the Pacific

Flying Over 10,000 Miles

Trippe and his party traveled 13,194 kilometers on this trial flight of the China-America direct route. With this test flight, the China-America line is fully completed. According to reports, there are 78 stations on the route from the United States to China, with the main landing stations including Honolulu and Midway Island. The distance from Los Angeles to Honolulu is 3,862 kilometers, from Honolulu to Midway Island is 2,220 kilometers, from Midway Island to Wake Island is 1,837 kilometers, from Wake Island to Guam is 2,860 kilometers, from Guam to the Philippines is 2,413 kilometers, from the Philippines to Hong Kong is 1,271 kilometers, and from Hong Kong to Shanghai is 1,448 kilometers, totaling 13,194 kilometers. Completing the entire route takes approximately twelve days.

Foreign Media Coverage

The Evening Post of America reported that the first group of passengers on the regular air route from the United States to the Far East will arrive at the Longhua Airport at approximately 4:30 PM today (the 24th). They crossed the Pacific Ocean on a Pan American Airlines aircraft from Alameda, California, passing through Honolulu, Midway Island, Wake Island, Guam, Manila, and Macau before arriving in Hong Kong. The flight from Hong Kong to Shanghai will be on a Douglas Dolphin aircraft of China National Aviation Corporation. Among them are Mr. and Mrs. Trippe, the General Manager of Pan American Airlines, Mr. Biggsby, the Vice President of the Far East of the company, Mr. and Mrs. Whitely, the Chairman of the Board of the company, Mr. Howard, the General Manager and Editor-in-Chief of the New York World-Telegram, and Mr. Morris, the Far East Manager of the Associated Press. The Trippes, the Whitelys, and Howard departed from California, while Biggsby and Morris joined in Manila. McGatto, the former Secretary of the Treasury during President Wilson's administration, went to Hong Kong to await the return of the Philippine Clipper to the United States and will take it back to the country. Mr. Rudd, the Manila Manager of Pan American Airlines, also attached to Hong Kong from Manila, but did not come to Shanghai. Today, two aircraft of China National Aviation Corporation will arrive at Longhua Airport from Hong Kong in the afternoon. One aircraft carrying passengers flying across the Pacific is expected to arrive at 4:30 PM, and the other is a regular Guangdong-Shanghai flight that stopped briefly in Hong Kong, arriving at approximately 3:30 PM, carrying Biggsby and ordinary passengers. The passengers flying across the Pacific will stay in Shanghai until tomorrow or the day after, taking a trip to the new capital and the ancient capital, and then returning to the United States via the original route. This is the first group of passengers flying the Pacific Ocean on a commercial aircraft to arrive in Shanghai. The Philippine Clipper aircraft previously only flew to Manila, but is now flying from Manila to Macau for the first time, and then to Hong Kong. The expansion of the trans-Pacific air route from Manila via Macau to Hong Kong is a new era for commercial aviation. Not only is it convenient for passengers, but also airmail between Shanghai and San Francisco can be accelerated. Previously, airmail from Shanghai to the United States had to be shipped to Manila and then transported by plane, but now the entire journey is by air, which will be much faster than before.

According to the National News Agency's dispatch from Shanghai on the 24th, Howard, the Editor-in-Chief of the New York World-Telegram, arrived at the Longhua seaplane port from Hong Kong on a China National Aviation Corporation aircraft at 4:00 PM this afternoon, making him one of the fastest people to travel from a major American city to a major Chinese city. Howard departed from New York, in the eastern United States, on a transcontinental aircraft on October 12th at 5:10 PM and flew to Alameda in the west. He then took the Philippine Clipper, participating in the first passenger flight across the Pacific Ocean.

Huang Fu's Illness Is Out of Danger

Due to the Treatment by Fan Shisheng, According to the Central News Agency, Huang Fu, the former Chairman of the Executive Yuan's Peiping Political Affairs Reorganization Committee, who was previously ill, has been out of danger after being treated by traditional Chinese medicine practitioner Fan Shisheng. However, after a long illness, he still needs time to recover. The Central News Agency reporter met with Huang's attendants yesterday and inquired about Huang's condition. It was said that Huang returned to Shanghai from Mogan Mountain in the summer, and his old illness relapsed. He was admitted to the Hong En Hospital for treatment. Because Huang's illness was very complicated, in order to understand his condition and diagnose the root cause, he underwent surgery in the hospital on September 14, and it was determined that Huang was suffering from liver cancer. However, there is no effective drug for liver cancer in modern global medicine. Afterwards, his consciousness became confused, and he was in critical condition. The doctors at the hospital believed that there was no hope of recovery. They then learned that traditional Chinese medicine practitioner Fan Shisheng was proficient in medicine. Through a friend's introduction, he flew from Lushan to Shanghai on September 28 to treat Huang, believing that there was still hope of recovery. He treated Huang twice a day. Currently, Huang's condition has gone from complex to simple, the dangerous period has passed, his consciousness has cleared, and his spirit has gradually recovered. He can now talk for one or two hours, which is a significant improvement compared to before. However, there is more than 2,000 units of fluid in Huang's abdomen (due to Huang absorbing approximately 900 to 1,000 units of water per day, while only 500 to 600 units are discharged, resulting in daily accumulation), which urgently needs to be drained. Therefore, Dr. Fan administered a diuretic (traditional Chinese medicine) on the morning of the 24th to drain the accumulated fluid, and then further treatment will be carried out. He will return to Lushan after he recovers. Fan formerly served as the commander of the 51st Division and other positions, and made contributions to the party and the country. He has a unique secret in medicine. Since resigning and practicing medicine, he has saved countless people and does not accept consultation fees. Madame Chiang Kai-shek, the wife of President Chiang, also suffered from an illness once before, which was cured by Fan's treatment.

Yikangyu Electrical Materials Store - Warehouse Accident Yesterday

The warehouse of Yikangyu Electrical Materials Store at No. 54 Ningbo Road in the French Concession, which is owned by Zheng Wenyi of Ningbo, employs an old clerk named Luo Quan. The fire was very fierce at the time, with black smoke rising straight up. The firefighters from the French Concession Songshan Road Fire Brigade rushed to the scene with their fire engines to put out the fire. It took about an hour to extinguish the blaze. Liu Zhenhuan Discusses His Thoughts on Adjusting Sino-Japanese Relations - If Japan Destroys Peace, China is Prepared to Defend Itself and Sacrifice

According to the Central News Agency, Mr. Liu Zhenhuan was summoned by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek from Guangdong to Shanghai. After Chairman Chiang returns to Nanjing from Shaanxi, he will go to Nanjing for an audience. Yesterday, Mr. Liu expressed his views on adjusting Sino-Japanese relations to Western reporters as follows: The recent tension in Sino-Japanese relations has aroused the attention and alarm of countries around the world. Recalling the September 18th Incident, I wrote to my Japanese friend, Mr. Inukai Tsuyoshi, urging the Japanese government to change its policy as soon as possible in order to maintain the friendship and diplomatic relations between the two countries for hundreds of years. Time flies, and five years have passed in the blink of an eye. In the past two months, Japan has once again used the Chengdu, Beihai, and Shanghai incidents as excuses to make deeper threats. My initial idea was that the international situation of the two major powers in East Asia is related to world peace. China has never given up the occupied four northeastern provinces, and it is by no means the result of a failed war. Unexpectedly, Japan misunderstood and mistakenly believed that the occupation of the four northeastern provinces was an indication that China was willing to give up. This is a great mistake. The rapid resolution of the recent Guangdong-Guangxi issue is enough to prove that the Chinese people are thoroughly aware that internal differences are far less tense than the mood of unanimous opposition to foreign countries. If Japan destroys peace, the Chinese government, under the unified situation, will lead 450 million people and prepare to sacrifice for self-defense. Japan may not be in an absolutely advantageous position. First of all, in terms of military affairs, China is fighting because it is oppressed, while Japan is fighting for aggression. The difference between righteousness and unrighteousness is obvious, which is already unfavorable. Moreover, China waits at ease for the enemy to exhaust itself, which is easier in strategy than Japan's laborious and long-distance expedition. In terms of economy, since China implemented the new currency policy, its financial foundation has become stable. Japan's national debt has exceeded 10 billion yuan, and this year's budget has reached a huge 3.6 billion yuan. Its financial groups are already unwilling to continually add to the huge military expenditure. Once something happens, it will inevitably be exhausted to cope with it. Moreover, Japan has always regarded China as its largest market, with annual trade with China exceeding 130 million yuan. The suspension of wartime trade is inevitable. This kind of loss will more easily affect its national economy. Under the circumstances of high tax barriers built by Britain and the United States, Japan's commercial protection law has sometimes completely failed. Where else can it be compensated? Moreover, during wartime, national industries will inevitably shift to military needs, and the unemployment problem will inevitably become more serious. In terms of diplomacy, Japan has become isolated since it withdrew from the League of Nations. Recently, the Anglo-Russian naval agreement has posed a major threat to Japan. The United States is making every effort to consolidate its defense zones in the Pacific and is accelerating the shipbuilding process. Japan's desire to compete with the United States for naval power is by no means permitted by its economic environment. As a result, it will have to deal with the Pacific defense with a situation of one against three, which may not be within its power. Therefore, from all aspects, Japan does not have full confidence in the war. Thinking for Japan, it should still regard Sino-Japanese co-existence and co-prosperity as the fundamental national policy. If it still insists on a tough stance and threatens in every possible way, it is tantamount to plunging China and Japan into a desperate situation of common destruction, which will only increase the tragedy in the history of the yellow race. People in the neighboring country with foresight should not do this. Diplomacy has now reached the final stage, and whether it is a disaster or a blessing depends entirely on the Japanese themselves.

Another piece of information is that Yang Hu, Commander of the Songhu Garrison, went to the Cangzhou Hotel around 11 o'clock yesterday morning to visit Mr. Liu and had a pleasant conversation.

Central Bank Exchange of Legal Tender Crowded - Scoundrels Seize the Opportunity to Deceive - Ge Zhenfang Brings 角币(Jiaobi, small change) Every Morning - Cheating in Short Amounts to Those Exchanging

Since the circulation of legal tender, the exchange affairs of the Central Bank have become busy. Every day from 9:00 am to 11:00 am, people come to exchange legal tender for 角票(Jiaopiao, small denomination banknotes) or to exchange 角票(Jiaopiao) for legal tender. Among these people, employees of cigarette and paper shops are the most numerous. There is a man named Ge Zhenfang from Hangzhou, who works at the Xiangfeng cigarette and paper shop at No. 94 Yan Hai Lane in Nanshi. Because he felt that this kind of exchange method could be used as an opportunity to deceive, he would bring hundreds of yuan of 角票(Jiaopiao) to the Central Bank every morning. When he saw someone exchanging legal tender for 角票(Jiaopiao), he would say to that person, "I am exchanging 角票(Jiaopiao) for legal tender. Since you want to exchange legal tender for 角票(Jiaopiao), you can exchange what you have for what I have, which is convenient for both of us. Isn't it better than waiting for a long time?" People who want to exchange 角票(Jiaopiao) all hope to complete the transaction quickly and do not want to wait for a long time, so they mostly followed Ge's words and exchanged with him. Ge would look at the amount needed by the other party, such as 50 yuan or 100 yuan, and then take out the 角票(Jiaopiao) from his bag and give it to them. The tickets were neatly stacked, with each stack being 5 yuan, 10 yuan, 20 yuan, etc. When Ge received the legal tender, he would leave without waiting for the other party to finish counting the money. Therefore, even if the exchanger later found that the amount of 角票(Jiaopiao) was less than the amount exchanged, there was no way to find Ge's whereabouts. The money was lost, and they could only sigh in vain. Ge, on the other hand, only had to lift a hand and make a profit several times higher than any other business. Therefore, he made this his regular business and was never seen through. At 10 o'clock in the morning the day before yesterday, Ge went to the exchange office of the Central Bank again. At that time, the people exchanging tickets were very crowded. There was a person who looked like a shop clerk who wanted to exchange 100 yuan of 角票(Jiaopiao). Ge used his old trick and accepted the 100 yuan of legal tender and gave him nine stacks of 角票(Jiaopiao), saying that one stack was 20 yuan. The shop clerk immediately checked and found that the total amount was only 65 yuan, 35 yuan less. At that time, Ge had not gone far and was caught up.

Ge was reprimanded loudly. Knowing that he was at fault, he did not dare to argue, admitted that the count was not clear, and made up the missing amount. He privately rejoiced that he had made up for the deficiency and that the secret would not be revealed. Who knew that among the crowd of ticket exchangers gathered there, there happened to be someone who had been deceived before? One was Qiu Jinsheng, a shop clerk from Mitsui 洋行(Trading Company), who went to the Central Bank on the 21st of this month to exchange 50 yuan of 角票(Jiaopiao). He met Ge there and exchanged with him. When he counted the money, he was 15 yuan short, and Ge had disappeared. Qiu had to

admit his bad luck. One was Shao Botang Shi Liangpu, employees of the Qianruihe Qianchanghe cigarette and paper shops on Xinyongan Street, who also went to the Central Bank on the 19th of this month to exchange 50 yuan of 角票(Jiaopiao). They also met Ge and exchanged with him, and they were 10 yuan short. Therefore, Qiu, Shao, and Shi surrounded Ge. However, at this time, the shop clerk had already made up for the missing amount and went home alone. Then, the gatekeeper of No. 84 of the bank, saw this situation, asked what had happened, and then took Ge to the General Patrol House. Detective Jiang Shangpei searched Ge and found 24 yuan of legal tender and 395 yuan of 角票(Jiaopiao). Together, they were sent to the First Special District Local Court yesterday morning. Judge Ye Shengchao interrogated them. Qian Xunjiu, a lawyer from the patrol house, stated the situation of the defendant's deception and requested that he be punished in accordance with Article 339 of the Criminal Law. However, he was still afraid that there were more than just three or four people who had been deceived, so he asked the court to postpone the case and allow the patrol house to conduct a more detailed investigation. The court then questioned Ge Zhenfang about the situation of the deception, ordered the defendant to be detained, and postponed the next hearing to the fourth.

Jianghai Steamer - Miscellaneous Notes on Accidents - Huashun Damaged

The Huashun Steamer of the Huasheng Steamship Company of this port was going to Wuhu to load grain and goods to be transported to Guangdong. It was once stranded at Yuxi Port on the opposite side of Wuhu. It was rescued to Wuhu to load all the goods and anchored in front of the Wuhu Customs to wait for customs clearance. Unexpectedly, the Zhenchang Steamer of the Yangzi Company came and suddenly collided with the left side of the Huashun Steamer, causing the iron plates to be bent and dented a lot. The hull was badly damaged, but there were goods inside the cabin, which had to be unloaded before inspection. Fortunately, the damaged part was still above the waterline, which did not hinder navigation.
